  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Innovation starts with people ✨ 

At NTT DATA Business Solutions, we know that diversity, equity, inclusion, and wellbeing (DEI&amp;W) are not temporary initiatives – they are a fundamental pillar of who we are and how we grow together. 🌍✨

Our  𝐃𝐄𝐈&amp;𝐖 𝐑𝐞𝐩𝐨𝐫𝐭 𝟐𝟎𝟐𝟒 showcases how we:
- Create a culture of 𝐛𝐞𝐥𝐨𝐧𝐠𝐢𝐧𝐠, 𝐯𝐚𝐥𝐮𝐞, 𝐚𝐧𝐝 𝐫𝐞𝐬𝐩𝐞𝐜𝐭, where every voice matters.
- Foster 𝐞𝐪𝐮𝐢𝐭𝐲 𝐚𝐧𝐝 𝐢𝐧𝐜𝐥𝐮𝐬𝐢𝐨𝐧 through global initiatives – from gender equality and LGBTQIA+ inclusion to disability awareness and cultural exchange.
- Support 𝐦𝐞𝐧𝐭𝐚𝐥 𝐡𝐞𝐚𝐥𝐭𝐡 𝐚𝐧𝐝 𝐰𝐞𝐥𝐥𝐛𝐞𝐢𝐧𝐠 with programs that span every stage of life, from starting a career to preparing for retirement.
- Build a truly 𝐠𝐥𝐨𝐛𝐚𝐥 𝐜𝐨𝐦𝐦𝐮𝐧𝐢𝐭𝐲 of colleagues across more than 30 countries, united by collaboration and shared values.

A special thank you goes to our colleagues and partners: every photo in this report captures our people and partners. Your authenticity and commitment bring our values to life every day. 🙏

Discover the full report here 👉 <a class="link" href="https://nttd.link/OxF5m?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://nttd.link/OxF5m</a>

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fdiversity&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Diversity</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fdeiw&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#DEIW</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fdeireport&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#DEIReport</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Finclusion&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Inclusion</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">𝐏𝐨𝐰𝐞𝐫𝐢𝐧𝐠 𝐭𝐡𝐞 𝐟𝐮𝐭𝐮𝐫𝐞 𝐰𝐢𝐭𝐡 𝐒𝐀𝐏 𝐂𝐥𝐨𝐮𝐝 𝐄𝐑𝐏 🔋⚡️The leading battery manufacturer <a class="link" href="https://at.linkedin.com/company/banner-group-power-company?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Banner Group</a> has taken an exciting leap forward by moving from a complex legacy system to a modern, cloud-based ERP.

Now, the German family-owned business is:
✅ Unlocking agility with streamlined standard processes
✅ Reducing overhead and boosting efficiency
✅ Building a secure, scalable foundation for future growth

“SAP is considered expensive, but for us, this has not proven to be the case thanks to the public cloud approach,” says <a class="link" href="https://at.linkedin.com/in/werner-t%C3%B6pfl-929a7bba?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Werner Töpfl</a>, Managing Director at Banner GmbH.

As their trusted partner, 𝐍𝐓𝐓 𝐃𝐀𝐓𝐀 𝐁𝐮𝐬𝐢𝐧𝐞𝐬𝐬 𝐒𝐨𝐥𝐮𝐭𝐢𝐨𝐧𝐬 guided the transformation end-to-end from planning to implementation, ensuring a smooth transition and maximizing business value. Or in Töpfl’s words: “It's like marriage – without the right partner, it won't work.”

Get energized and read the full story here 👉  <a class="link" href="https://nttd.link/TrNVc?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://nttd.link/TrNVc</a>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">“Innovation has always been a key part of <a class="link" href="https://no.linkedin.com/company/ulstein?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>ULSTEIN</a> Group, and data is becoming increasingly important to drive that innovation”, says Johannes Volle, Chief Financial Officer at the leading Norwegian provider of ship designs, shipbuilding, and maritime system solutions.

Together with us, they have developed an Internet of Things (IoT) solution, aiming to offer a completely new experience for skippers: Information from ship operations is collected in a “blue box” on board and sent to the cloud to optimize machines with data-driven insights.

The solution is based on our momenttum platform, a strong basis for collecting and processing a wide range of data, which has been tried and tested over many years. 

Dive deeper into the data ocean and see digital twins of ships come alive!     <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">”𝐓𝐡𝐞 𝐜𝐡𝐞𝐦𝐢𝐬𝐭𝐫𝐲 𝐰𝐚𝐬 𝐫𝐢𝐠𝐡𝐭.” 🧪✨

<a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/company/tib-chemicals?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>TIB Chemicals</a>, a global chemical company based in Germany, selected us from eight other service providers to modernize its operations and stay ahead in a rapidly changing market. 

By implementing 𝐒𝐀𝐏 ���𝐥𝐨𝐮𝐝 𝐄𝐑𝐏, the company streamlines processes, benefits from automatic updates, and leverages best practices for a faster and more efficient implementation. With 𝐒𝐀𝐏 𝐆𝐥𝐨𝐛𝐚𝐥 𝐓𝐫𝐚𝐝𝐞 𝐒𝐞𝐫𝐯𝐢𝐜𝐞𝐬 (𝐆𝐓𝐒), they bundle compliance, customs, preferences, and Intrastat in one system. This allows international trade processes to be managed securely, efficiently, and automatically.

This strategic move not only ensures future-ready, scalable operations but also underscores the importance of selecting a partner that combines expertise with collaboration – essential for projects of this scale.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">“We really appreciate how NTT DATA Business Solutions responds to our requirements and needs", says <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/annmertens-?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Ann Mertens</a>, Sustainability Officer at <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/company/mosca-gmbh?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mosca GmbH</a>, after the successful go-live of their new scalable, SAP-integrated sustainability management application. 

The manufacturer of packaging systems has transitioned from manual Excel CO₂e calculations to 𝐒𝐮𝐬𝐭𝐚𝐢𝐧𝐚𝐛𝐢𝐥𝐢𝐭𝐲 𝐃𝐚𝐭𝐚 𝐒𝐢𝐦𝐩𝐥𝐢𝐟𝐢𝐞𝐝, our solution to streamline and automate sustainability data management.

Now they benefit from:
🌳 Automated CO₂e footprint calculations in line with Greenhouse Gas (GHG) Protocol standards and the Corporate Sustainability Reporting Directive (CSRD)
🌳 A single source of truth via sustainability attributes embedded in SAP master data
🌳 Flexible data sourcing, from Ecoinvent to supplier-specific inputs

Together, we achieved a fast, future-proof implementation by starting with strap products, now scaling the solution toward complete machinery integration. This evolution frees the team to focus on data quality and strategic insight, paving the way for scalable, robust sustainability reporting.

Read the full story here 👉 <a class="link" href="https://nttd.link/DJLav?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://nttd.link/DJLav</a>

<a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/company/sap?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SAP</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsustainability&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Sustainability</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fco2&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#CO2</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsustainabilitymanagement&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SustainabilityManagement</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">📊 𝐀𝐧𝐧𝐮𝐚𝐥 𝐑𝐞𝐩𝐨𝐫𝐭 𝟐𝟎𝟐𝟒/𝟐𝟓 – record revenue of €1.85 billion (+14.7%), continued organic growth with 16,700+ colleagues in 30 countries, and strong momentum across all business areas. ✨

After almost three months in her new role as CFO, <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/nicolacl?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Nicola Czymek-Lauer</a> personal assessment is just as positive as the figures in the report: “In my view, NTT DATA Business Solutions combines the best of both worlds: a clear focus on performance and growth orientation combined with a long-term entrepreneurial mindset. It’s a great mix. Our parent company NTT DATA gives us considerable freedom and supports our growth strategy, which is geared toward sustainable success.”

In June 2025, Nicola succeeded <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/juergen-puerzer-04465272?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Juergen Puerzer</a> as our new CFO. Reflecting on the transition, she notes: “As CFO, Jürgen has laid several important foundations. I am very much looking forward to continuing and developing his successful work together with the entire team – on the cloud-based ERP system and beyond.”

Discover in our Annual Report 2024/25 the goals Nicola has set to drive sustainable growth, innovation, and long-term impact 👉 <a class="link" href="https://nttd.link/GmiOw?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://nttd.link/GmiOw</a>

What a finish! 🏆 After five grueling days and more than 3,000 kilometers through the Australian outback, the <a class="link" href="https://nl.linkedin.com/company/brunel-solar-team?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Brunel Solar Team</a> crossed the finish line in Adelaide first – winning the World Solar Challenge 2025 and securing their eighth world title in solar racing.
 
We followed the race with excitement and are proud to celebrate their victory. As a technology partner, our role went beyond sponsorship. Together, we introduced innovations like GenAI-powered documentation search and Digital Twin simulations – making Nuna 13 smarter, faster, and safer on the road to success.
